This highlights a key limitation of the mirror circuit approach: while it is simple and requires no classical simulation, it does not scale well to large or deep circuits, where both methods are pushed close to the noise floor and the small surviving signal is dominated by accumulated error."],"className":"group paragraph-el text-text-primary mx-0"}]
